</div>
			<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Pesticide</h1>
									<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
									<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
								<div id="contentSub"></div>
												<div id="jump-to-nav" class="mw-jump">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
				</div>
				<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Cropduster_spraying_pesticides.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Cropduster_spraying_pesticides.jpg/220px-Cropduster_spraying_pesticides.jpg" width="220" height="325" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Cropduster_spraying_pesticides.jpg/330px-Cropduster_spraying_pesticides.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/5/5e/Cropduster_spraying_pesticides.jpg 2x" data-file-width="433" data-file-height="640" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Cropduster_spraying_pesticides.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
A <a href="/wiki/Crop-duster" class="mw-redirect" title="Crop-duster">crop-duster</a> spraying pesticide on a field</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Lite-Trac_Crop_Sprayer.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Lite-Trac_Crop_Sprayer.jpg/220px-Lite-Trac_Crop_Sprayer.jpg" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Lite-Trac_Crop_Sprayer.jpg/330px-Lite-Trac_Crop_Sprayer.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Lite-Trac_Crop_Sprayer.jpg/440px-Lite-Trac_Crop_Sprayer.jpg 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="675" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Lite-Trac_Crop_Sprayer.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
A <a href="/wiki/Lite-Trac" title="Lite-Trac">Lite-Trac</a> four-wheeled self-propelled crop sprayer spraying pesticide on a field</div>
</div>
</div>
<p><b>Pesticides</b> are substances that are meant to control <a href="/wiki/Pest_(animal)" class="mw-redirect" title="Pest (animal)">pests</a> or weeds.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> The term pesticide includes all of the following: <a href="/wiki/Herbicide" title="Herbicide">herbicide</a>, <a href="/wiki/Insecticide" title="Insecticide">insecticide</a>, <a href="/wiki/Insect_growth_regulator" title="Insect growth regulator">insect growth regulator</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nematicide" title="Nematicide">nematicide</a>, termiticide, <a href="/wiki/Molluscicide" title="Molluscicide">molluscicide</a>, <a href="/wiki/Piscicide" title="Piscicide">piscicide</a>, <a href="/wiki/Avicide" title="Avicide">avicide</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rodenticide" title="Rodenticide">rodenticide</a>, predacide, <a href="/wiki/Bactericide" title="Bactericide">bactericide</a>, <a href="/wiki/Insect_repellent" title="Insect repellent">insect repellent</a>, <a href="/wiki/Animal_repellent" title="Animal repellent">animal repellent</a>, <a href="/wiki/Antimicrobial" title="Antimicrobial">antimicrobial</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fungicide" title="Fungicide">fungicide</a>, <a href="/wiki/Disinfectant" title="Disinfectant">disinfectant</a> (antimicrobial), and <a href="/wiki/Sanitizer" class="mw-redirect" title="Sanitizer">sanitizer</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> The most common of these are herbicides which account for approximately 80% of all pesticide use.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> Most pesticides are intended to serve as plant protection products (also known as crop protection products), which in general, protect plants from <a href="/wiki/Weed" title="Weed">weeds</a>, fungi, or <a href="/wiki/Insect" title="Insect">insects</a>.</p>
<p>In general, a pesticide is a chemical or biological agent (such as a <a href="/wiki/Virus" title="Virus">virus</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bacterium" class="mw-redirect" title="Bacterium">bacterium</a>, antimicrobial, or disinfectant) that deters, incapacitates, kills, or otherwise discourages pests. Target pests can include insects, plant <a href="/wiki/Pathogen" title="Pathogen">pathogens</a>, weeds, <a href="/wiki/Mollusca" title="Mollusca">mollusks</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bird" title="Bird">birds</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mammal" title="Mammal">mammals</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fish" title="Fish">fish</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nematode" title="Nematode">nematodes</a> (<a href="/wiki/Roundworm" class="mw-redirect" title="Roundworm">roundworms</a>), and <a href="/wiki/Microbe" class="mw-redirect" title="Microbe">microbes</a> that destroy property, cause nuisance, or spread disease, or are disease <a href="/wiki/Vector_(epidemiology)" title="Vector (epidemiology)">vectors</a>. Although pesticides have benefits, some also have drawbacks, such as potential toxicity to humans and other species. According to the <a href="/wiki/Stockholm_Convention_on_Persistent_Organic_Pollutants" title="Stockholm Convention on Persistent Organic Pollutants">Stockholm Convention on Persistent Organic Pollutants</a>, 9 of the 12 most dangerous and persistent <a href="/wiki/Organic_chemicals" class="mw-redirect" title="Organic chemicals">organic chemicals</a> are organochlorine pesticides.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Gilden_RC.2C_Huffling_K.2C_Sattler_B_2010_103.E2.80.9310_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Gilden_RC.2C_Huffling_K.2C_Sattler_B_2010_103.E2.80.9310-5">[5]</a></sup></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Definition">Definition</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Pesticide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Definition">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="wikitable" style="float: right; margin-left:15px; text-align:center">
<tr>
